vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span> and compute this way:</em></p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>8</mn><msup><mn>9</mn><mn>2</mn></msup><msub><mo>‚â°</mo><mn>99</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo>‚àí</mo><mn>10</mn><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>100</mn><msub><mo>‚â°</mo><mn>99</mn></msub><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
89^{2} \equiv_{99}(-10)^{2}=100 \equiv_{99} 1
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.01411em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord">8</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">9</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.864108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel">‚â°</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">9</span><span class="mord mtight">9</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.11411em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">‚àí</span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.864108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.79444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel">‚â°</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">9</span><span class="mord mtight">9</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><em>You can compute either of these examples the ‚Äúhard way‚Äù to verify that these shortcuts lead to the correct answer.</em></p>
<p>Since addition, subtraction, and multiplication are defined over the integers (<em>i.e.</em>, adding/subtracting/multiplying integers always results in an integer), these kinds of tricks can be helpful.</p>
<p>On the other hand, dividing integers doesn‚Äôt always result in an integer. Does it make sense to use division when working mod <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">n</span></span></span></span></span>, where the result always has to lie in <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="double-struck">Z</mi><mi>n</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{Z}_n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.83889em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">Z</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.151392em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>? We will answer this question later in the book.</p>
<h2 id="strings-a-namech0section3a">0.3	Strings <a></a></h2>
<p>We write <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle><mo separator="true">,</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>1</mn></mstyle><msup><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mi>n</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{\textcolor{brown}{0}, \textcolor{brown}{1}\}^n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">n</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> to denote the set of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">n</span></span></span></span></span>-bit binary strings, and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle><mo separator="true">,</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>1</mn></mstyle><msup><mo stretchy="false">}</mo><mo>‚àó</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{\textcolor{brown}{0}, \textcolor{brown}{1}\}^{*}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.688696em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">‚àó</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> to denote the set of all (finite-length) binary strings. When <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span> is a string of bits, we write <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>‚à£</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>‚à£</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mid x \mid</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span></span></span></span></span> to denote the length (in bits) of that string, and we write <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mover accent="true"><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="true">‚Äæ</mo></mover></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\overline{x}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.63056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord overline"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.63056em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.55056em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="overline-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> to denote the result of flipping every bit in <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span>. When it‚Äôs clear from context that we‚Äôre talking about strings instead of numbers, we write <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle><mi>n</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{0}^n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.664392em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">n</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>1</mn></mstyle><mi>n</mi></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{1}^n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.664392em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.664392em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">n</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> to denote strings of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">n</span></span></span></span></span> zeroes and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">n</span></span></span></span></span> ones, respectively (rather than the result of raising the <em>integers</em> <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span> or <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span> to the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">n</span></span></span></span></span> power). As you might have noticed, I also try to use a different font and color for characters (including bits, anything that could be used to build a string through concatenation) vs. integers.</p>
<p><strong>Definition 0.5 (<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>‚äï</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\oplus</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord">‚äï</span></span></span></span></span>, XOR)</strong><br>
<em>When <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span> are strings of the same length, we write <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \oplus y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span> to denote the bitwise exclusive-or (XOR) of the two strings. The expression <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \oplus y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span> is generally not defined when the strings are different lengths, but in rare occasions it is useful to consider the shorter string being padded with <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{0}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span></span></span></span></span>s. When that‚Äôs the case, we must have an explicit convention about whether the shorter string is padded with leading <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{0}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span></span></span></span></span>s or trailing <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{0}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span></span></span></span></span>s.</em></p>
<p>For example, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0011</mn></mstyle><mo>‚äï</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0101</mn></mstyle><mo>=</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0110</mn></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{0011} \oplus \textcolor{brown}{0101} = \textcolor{brown}{0110}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.72777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span></span></span></span></span>. The following facts about the XOR operation are frequently useful:</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.15999999999999992em" columnalign="right left left left" columnspacing="1em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>000</mn><mo>‚ãØ</mo></mstyle></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mtext>XOR‚Äôing&nbsp;a&nbsp;string&nbsp;with&nbsp;itself&nbsp;results&nbsp;in&nbsp;zeroes.</mtext></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>000</mn><mo>‚ãØ</mo></mstyle></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mtext>XOR‚Äôing&nbsp;with&nbsp;zeroes&nbsp;has&nbsp;no&nbsp;effect.</mtext></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>111</mn><mo>‚ãØ</mo></mstyle></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mover accent="true"><mi>x</mi><mo>Àâ</mo></mover></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mtext>XOR‚Äôing&nbsp;with&nbsp;ones&nbsp;flips&nbsp;every&nbsp;bit.</mtext></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>y</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mtext>XOR&nbsp;is&nbsp;symmetric.</mtext></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>z</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="false"><mtext>XOR&nbsp;is&nbsp;associative.</mtext></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
\begin{array}{rlll}
x \oplus x &amp;=\textcolor{brown}{000 \cdots} &amp; \text{XOR‚Äôing a string with itself results in zeroes.} \\
x \oplus \textcolor{brown}{000 \cdots} &amp;=x  &amp; \text{XOR‚Äôing with zeroes has no effect.}\\
x \oplus \textcolor{brown}{111 \cdots} &amp;=\bar{x} &amp; \text{XOR‚Äôing with ones flips every bit.} \\
x \oplus y &amp;=y \oplus x &amp; \text{XOR is symmetric.} \\
(x \oplus y) \oplus z &amp;=x \oplus(y \oplus z) &amp; \text{XOR is associative.} \\
\end{array}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 6em; vertical-align: -2.75em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.25em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.41em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.21em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner" style="color: brown;">‚ãØ</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.01em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner" style="color: brown;">‚ãØ</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.81em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -0.61em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.04398em;">z</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.75em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.25em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.41em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner" style="color: brown;">‚ãØ</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.21em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.01em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord accent"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.56778em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="accent-body" style="left: -0.22222em;">Àâ</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.81em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -0.61em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.75em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 3.25em;"><span class="" style="top: -5.41em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">XOR‚Äôing&nbsp;a&nbsp;string&nbsp;with&nbsp;itself&nbsp;results&nbsp;in&nbsp;zeroes.</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -4.21em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">XOR‚Äôing&nbsp;with&nbsp;zeroes&nbsp;has&nbsp;no&nbsp;effect.</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -3.01em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">XOR‚Äôing&nbsp;with&nbsp;ones&nbsp;flips&nbsp;every&nbsp;bit.</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -1.81em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">XOR&nbsp;is&nbsp;symmetric.</span></span></span></span><span class="" style="top: -0.61em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">XOR&nbsp;is&nbsp;associative.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 2.75em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>See if you can use these properties to derive the very useful fact below:</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>c</mi><mo>‚ü∫</mo><mi>b</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>c</mi><mo>‚ü∫</mo><mi>c</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>b</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
a = b \oplus c \Longleftrightarrow b = a \oplus c \Longleftrightarrow c = a \oplus b.
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.549em; vertical-align: -0.024em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚ü∫</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.549em; vertical-align: -0.024em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚ü∫</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">c</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">b</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>There are a few ways to think about XOR that may help you in this class:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Bit-flipping:</strong> Note that XOR‚Äôing a bit with <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>0</mn></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{0}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span></span></span></span></span> has no effect, while XOR‚Äôing with <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>1</mn></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{1}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span></span></span></span></span> flips that bit. You can think of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \oplus y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span> as: ‚Äústarting with <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span>, flip the bits at all the positions where <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span> has a <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>1</mn></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{1}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span></span></span></span></span>.‚Äù So if <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span> is all <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>1</mn></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\textcolor{brown}{1}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span></span></span></span></span>‚Äôs, then <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \oplus y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span> gives the bitwise-complement of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span>. If <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo>=</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>1010</mn><mo>‚ãØ</mo></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y = \textcolor{brown}{1010 \cdots}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner" style="color: brown;">‚ãØ</span></span></span></span></span> then <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \oplus y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span> means ‚Äú(the result of) flipping every other bit in <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span>.‚Äù<br>
Many concepts in this course can be understood in terms of bit-flipping. For example, we might ask ‚Äúwhat happens when I flip the first bit of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span> and send it into the algorithm?‚Äù This kind of question could also be phrased as ‚Äúwhat happens when I send <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mstyle mathcolor="brown"><mn>1000</mn><mo>‚ãØ</mo></mstyle></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \oplus \textcolor{brown}{1000 \cdots}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">1</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mord" style="color: brown;">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.166667em;"></span><span class="minner" style="color: brown;">‚ãØ</span></span></span></span></span> into the algorithm?‚Äù Usually there is nothing special about flipping just the first bit of a string, so it will often be quite reasonable to generalize the question as ‚Äúwhat happens when I send <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \oplus y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span> into the algorithm, for an arbitrary (not-all-zeroes) string <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span>?‚Äù</li>
<li><strong>Addition mod-2:</strong> XOR is just addition mod <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span></span></span></span></span> in every bit. This way of thinking about XOR helps to explain why ‚Äúalgebraic‚Äù things like <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>z</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(x \oplus y) \oplus z = x \oplus (y \oplus z)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> are true. They are true for addition, so they are true for XOR.<br>
This also might help you remember why <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚äï</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \oplus x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">‚äï</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span> is all zeroes. If instead of XOR we used addition, we would surely write <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>+</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x + x = 2x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.66666em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span>. Since <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><msub><mo>‚â°</mo><mn>2</mn></msub><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2 \equiv_2 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.79444em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel">‚â°</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>, we get that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span> is congruent to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn><mi>x</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0x = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span></span></span></span></span>.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Definition 0.6 (<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">‚à£</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">‚à£</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">||</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">‚à£</span><span class="mord">‚à£</span></span></span></span></span>, concatenation)</strong><br>
<em>We write <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">‚à£</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">‚à£</mi><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x || y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mord">‚à£</span><span class="mord">‚à£</span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span> to denote the result of <strong>concatenating</strong> <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span></em>.</p>
<h2 id="functions-a-namech0section4a">0.4	Functions <a></a></h2>
<p>Let <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span></span> be finite sets. A function <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>:</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>‚Üí</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f : X  \to Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚Üí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span></span> is:</p>
<p><strong>injective</strong> (1-to-1) if it maps distinct inputs to distinct outputs. Formally: <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">‚â†</mi><msup><mi>x</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">‚Ä≤</mo></msup><mo>‚áí</mo><mi>f</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">‚â†</mi><mi>f</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>x</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">‚Ä≤</mo></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \neq x' \Rightarrow f(x) \neq f(x')</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.69444em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mrel">ÓÄ†</span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.19444em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">‚Ä≤</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚áí</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.69444em;"><span class="" style="top: -3em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;"></span><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mrel">ÓÄ†</span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.19444em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.00189em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">‚Ä≤</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>. If there is an injective function from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span></span>, then we must have <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>‚à£</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo>‚à£</mo><mo>‚â•</mo><mo>‚à£</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>‚à£</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mid Y \mid \geq \mid X \mid</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77194em; vertical-align: -0.13597em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚â•</span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p><strong>surjective</strong> (onto) if every element in <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span></span> is a possible output of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>f</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span></span></span></span></span>. Formally: for all <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo>‚àà</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y \in Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.73354em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚àà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span></span> there exists an <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚àà</mo><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \in X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5782em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚àà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> with <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f(x) = y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span></span>. If there is a surjective function from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span></span>, then we must have <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>‚à£</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo>‚à£</mo><mo>‚â§</mo><mo>‚à£</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>‚à£</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mid Y \mid \leq \mid X \mid</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77194em; vertical-align: -0.13597em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚â§</span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p><strong>bijective</strong> (1-to-1 correspondence) if <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>f</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.10764em;">f</span></span></span></span></span> is both injective and surjective. If there is a bijective function from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span></span>, then we must have <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>‚à£</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>‚à£</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>‚à£</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo>‚à£</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mid X \mid = \mid Y \mid</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.36687em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚à£</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<h2 id="probability">0.5	Probability</h2>
<p><strong>Definition 0.7 (Distribution)</strong><br>
<em>A <strong>(discrete) probability distribution</strong> over a set <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> of <strong>outcomes</strong> is usually written as a function</em> ‚ÄúPr‚Äù <em>that associates each outcome <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚àà</mo><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \in X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5782em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚àà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> with a probability</em> Pr[x]. <em>We often say that the distribution <strong>assigns</strong> probability</em> Pr[x] <em>to outcome <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span></span></span></span></span></em>.</p>
<p><em>For each outcome <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚àà</mo><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x \in X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5782em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚àà</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span>, the probability distribution must satisfy the condition <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn><mo>‚â§</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0 \leq</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.78041em; vertical-align: -0.13597em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚â§</span></span></span></span></span></em> Pr[x] <em><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>‚â§</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\leq 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.77194em; vertical-align: -0.13597em;"></span><span class="mrel">‚â§</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.277778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span>. Additionally, the sum of all probabilities <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mo>‚àë</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>‚àà</mo><mi>X</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\sum_{x \in X}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.07708em; vertical-align: -0.32708em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="position: relative; top: -5e-06em;">‚àë</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.178621em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.40029em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathdefault mtight">x</span><span class="mrel mtight">‚àà</span><span class="mord mathdefault mtight" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">‚Äã</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.32708em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></em> Pr[x] <em>must equal <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span></em>.</p>
<p><strong>Definition 0.8 (Uniform)</strong><br>
<em>A special distribution is the <strong>uniform distribution</strong> over a finite set <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;
